<script>
    var handleRedirections = (function(){
        if(window.self === window.top){
            var destinationEnv = window.location.host.indexOf('dev') >= 0 ? 'www.dev.' : window.location.host.indexOf('qa') >= 0 ? 'www.qa.' : '';
            var ausLocale = window.location.host.indexOf('au') === 0 ? '/au/en' : '';
            var destination = 'ring.com';
            var destinationEndpoint = 'ring.com' + ausLocale;

            //send specific paths to belem /collections/all-products, add more here if needed
            var defaultRedirects = [
                '/',
                '/collections',
                '/collections/',
                '/collections/all',
                '/collections/all/',
                '/products',
                '/products/'
            ];
            var path = window.location.pathname;
            var normalizedPath = path.charAt(path.length - 1) !== '/' ? path + '/' : path;
            var pathCheck = defaultRedirects.indexOf(normalizedPath);
            var params = window.location.search ? '/' + window.location.search : '';
            if(document.referrer) {
              const referrerHostname = document.referrer.match(/(.+?):\/\/.+?(\/|$)/g);
              if(referrerHostname) {
                const originalReferrerQuery = 'original_referrer=' + encodeURIComponent(referrerHostname[0]);
                params += params ? '&' + originalReferrerQuery : '/?' + originalReferrerQuery;
              }
            }
            var ausMatch = window.location.host.indexOf('au');
            var collectionsMatch = window.location.pathname.match(/(\/collections.*)/gi);
            var productsMatch = window.location.pathname.match(/(\/products.*)/gi);

            // Product & Collections Redirects
            if(pathCheck !== -1){
                var route = path === '/' ? '' : '/collections/all-products';
                window.location.replace('https://' + destinationEnv + destinationEndpoint + route + params);
            } else if(collectionsMatch){
              var productURL = normalizedPath.toString();
              const regex = /(\/collections\/.*?\/)/gm;
              cleanURL = productURL.split(regex)[2];
              window.location.replace('https://' + destinationEnv + destination + ausLocale + '/' + productURL.split(regex)[2] + params);
            } else if(productsMatch){
                window.location.replace('https://' + destinationEnv + destination + ausLocale +  productsMatch[0] + params);
            } else {
                return;
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function ($) {
        var $modal = $('#product_detail_modal');

        $modal.on('CLOSE_MODAL', function closeModalHandler() {
            $(this).fadeOut(100);
        });

        // Attaches close behaviour
        $('#modal_close_product_detail_modal, .ring-modal__backdrop').click(function () {
            $modal.trigger('CLOSE_MODAL');
        });
    })(jQuery);
</script>

<script>
	Shopify.AjaxifyCart = (function($) {
	  
	  // Some configuration options.
	  // I have separated what you will never need to change from what
	  // you might change.
	  
	  var _config = {
	    
	    // What you might want to change
	    addToCartBtnLabel:             'Add to cart',
	    addedToCartBtnLabel:           'Thank you!',
	    addingToCartBtnLabel:          'Adding...',
	    soldOutBtnLabel:               'Sold Out',
	    howLongTillBtnReturnsToNormal: 1000, // in milliseconds.
	    cartCountSelector:             '.cart-count, #cart-count a:first, #gocart p a, #cart .checkout em, .item-count, #CartCount',
	    cartTotalSelector:             '#cart-price',
	    // 'aboveForm' for top of add to cart form, 
	    // 'belowForm' for below the add to cart form, and 
	    // 'nextButton' for next to add to cart button.
	    feedbackPosition:              'nextButton',
	    
	    // What you will never need to change
	    addToCartBtnSelector:          '[type="submit"]',
	    addToCartFormSelector:         'form[action="/cart/add"]',
	    shopifyAjaxAddURL:             '/cart/add.js',
	    shopifyAjaxCartURL:            '/cart.js'
	  };
	  
	  // We need some feedback when adding an item to the cart.
	  // Here it is.  
	  var _showFeedback = function(success, html, $addToCartForm) {
      if (_config.feedbackPosition === 'noFeedback') return;
	    $('.ajaxified-cart-feedback').remove();
	    var feedback = '<p class="ajaxified-cart-feedback ' + success + '">' + html + '</p>';
	    switch (_config.feedbackPosition) {
	      case 'aboveForm':
	        $addToCartForm.before(feedback);
	        break;
	      case 'belowForm':
	        $addToCartForm.after(feedback);
	        break;
	      case 'nextButton':
	      default:
	        $addToCartForm.find(_config.addToCartBtnSelector).after(feedback);
	        break;   
	    }
	    // If you use animate.css
	    // $('.ajaxified-cart-feedback').addClass('animated bounceInDown');
	    $('.ajaxified-cart-feedback').slideDown();
	  };
	  var _setText = function($button, label) {
	    if ($button.children().length) {
	      $button.children().each(function() {
	        if ($.trim($(this).text()) !== '') {
	          $(this).text(label);
	        }
	      });
	    }
	    else {
	      $button.val(label).text(label);
	    }
	  };

	  var addToCart = function(e, conf) {
      e && e.preventDefault();
      var $addToCartForm = $(this);
      var data = {};
      if (!conf.product) {
        data = $addToCartForm.serialize();
      } else {
        data = conf.product;
      }
      var $addToCartBtn = $addToCartForm.find(conf.addToCartBtnSelector);

      _setText($addToCartBtn, conf.addingToCartBtnLabel);
      $addToCartBtn.addClass('disabled').prop('disabled', true);
      // Add to cart.
      $.ajax({
        url: conf.shopifyAjaxAddURL,
        dataType: 'json',
        type: 'post',
        data,
        success: function(itemData) {
          // Re-enable add to cart button.
          $addToCartBtn.addClass('inverted');
          _setText($addToCartBtn, conf.addedToCartBtnLabel);
          _showFeedback('success','<i class="fa fa-check"></i> Added to cart! <a href="/cart">View cart</a>.',$addToCartForm);
          window.setTimeout(function(){
            $addToCartBtn.prop('disabled', false).removeClass('disabled').removeClass('inverted');
            _setText($addToCartBtn,conf.addToCartBtnLabel);
          }, conf.howLongTillBtnReturnsToNormal);
          // Update cart count and show cart link.
          $.getJSON(conf.shopifyAjaxCartURL, function(cart) {
            
            $(cart.items).each(function(i,v){
              var found = false;
              $('#shopify-section-header .item').each(function(p,t){
                if($(this).data('variant') == v.variant_id){
                  $(this).find('.qty').text(v.quantity)
                  found = true;
                }
              })
              if(!found){
                $('#shopify-section-header .items').prepend('<a href="'+v.url+'"><div class="item" data-variant="'+v.variant_id+'"><div class="img"><img class="cart__image" src="'+v.image+'" alt="'+v.title+'"></div><div><span class="title">'+v.title+'</span><br>QTY: <span class="qty">'+v.quantity+'</span></div><div></div></div></a>')
              }
            })
            $('#mini-cart').stop(true,true).fadeIn(200).delay(5000).fadeOut(500);

            
            if (conf.cartCountSelector && $(conf.cartCountSelector).size()) {
              var value = $(conf.cartCountSelector).html() || '0';
              $(conf.cartCountSelector).html(value.replace(/[0-9]+/,cart.item_count)).removeClass('hidden-count');
            }
            if (conf.cartTotalSelector && $(conf.cartTotalSelector).size()) {
              if (typeof Currency !== 'undefined' && typeof Currency.moneyFormats !== 'undefined') {
                var newCurrency = '';
                if ($('[name="currencies"]').size()) {
                  newCurrency = $('[name="currencies"]').val();
                }
                else if ($('#currencies span.selected').size()) {
                  newCurrency = $('#currencies span.selected').attr('data-currency');
                }
                if (newCurrency) {
                  $(conf.cartTotalSelector).html('<span class=money>' + Shopify.formatMoney(Currency.convert(cart.total_price, "USD", newCurrency), Currency.money_format[newCurrency]) + '</span>');
                } 
                else {
                  $(conf.cartTotalSelector).html(Shopify.formatMoney(cart.total_price, "${{amount}}"));
                }
              }
              else {
                $(conf.cartTotalSelector).html(Shopify.formatMoney(cart.total_price, "${{amount}}"));
              }
            };
          });        
        }, 
        error: function(XMLHttpRequest) {
          var response = eval('(' + XMLHttpRequest.responseText + ')');
          response = response.description;
          if (response.slice(0,4) === 'All ') {
            _showFeedback('error', response.replace('All 1 ', 'All '), $addToCartForm);
            $addToCartBtn.prop('disabled', false);
            _setText($addToCartBtn, _config.soldOutBtnLabel);
            $addToCartBtn.prop('disabled',true);
          }
          else {
            _showFeedback('error', '<i class="fa fa-warning"></i> ' + response, $addToCartForm);
            $addToCartBtn.prop('disabled', false).removeClass('disabled');
            _setText($addToCartBtn, _config.addToCartBtnLabel);
          }
        }
      });   
      return false;    
    }

	  var _init = function() {   
	    $(document).ready(function() { 
	      $(_config.addToCartFormSelector).submit(addToCart);
	    });
	  };
	  return {
	    init: function(params) {
	        // Configuration
	        params = params || {};
	        // Merging with defaults.
	        $.extend(_config, params);
	        // Action
	        $(function() {
	          _init();
	        });
	    },    
	    getConfig: function() {
	      return _config;
	    },
      addToCart: function(params) {
        config = Object.assign(_config, params);
        addToCart.call(this, null, config);
      },
	  }  
	})(jQuery);
	
	Shopify.AjaxifyCart.init();
	</script>

	<div id="shopify-section-ajaxify-cart" class="shopify-section">
<script>
	Shopify.AjaxifyCart = (function($) {
	  
	  // Some configuration options.
	  // I have separated what you will never need to change from what
	  // you might change.
	  
	  var _config = {
	    
	    // What you might want to change
	    addToCartBtnLabel:             'Add to cart',
	    addedToCartBtnLabel:           'Thank you!',
	    addingToCartBtnLabel:          'Adding...',
	    soldOutBtnLabel:               'Sold Out',
	    howLongTillBtnReturnsToNormal: 1000, // in milliseconds.
	    cartCountSelector:             '.cart-count, #cart-count a:first, #gocart p a, #cart .checkout em, .item-count, #CartCount',
	    cartTotalSelector:             '#cart-price',
	    // 'aboveForm' for top of add to cart form, 
	    // 'belowForm' for below the add to cart form, and 
	    // 'nextButton' for next to add to cart button.
	    feedbackPosition:              'beforeButton',
	    
	    // What you will never need to change
	    addToCartBtnSelector:          '[type="submit"]',
	    addToCartFormSelector:         'form[action="/cart/add"]',
	    shopifyAjaxAddURL:             '/cart/add.js',
	    shopifyAjaxCartURL:            '/cart.js'
	  };
	  
	  // We need some feedback when adding an item to the cart.
	  // Here it is.  
	  var _showFeedback = function(success, html, $addToCartForm) {
      if (_config.feedbackPosition === 'noFeedback') return;
	    $('.ajaxified-cart-feedback').remove();
	    var feedback = '<p class="ajaxified-cart-feedback ' + success + '">' + html + '</p>';
	    switch (_config.feedbackPosition) {
	      case 'aboveForm':
	        $addToCartForm.before(feedback);
	        break;
	      case 'belowForm':
	        $addToCartForm.after(feedback);
	        break;
        case 'beforeButton':
	      	$addToCartForm.find(_config.addToCartBtnSelector).before(feedback);
	      	break;
	      case 'nextButton':
	      default:
	        $addToCartForm.find(_config.addToCartBtnSelector).after(feedback);
	        break;   
	    }
	    // If you use animate.css
	    // $('.ajaxified-cart-feedback').addClass('animated bounceInDown');
	    $('.ajaxified-cart-feedback').slideDown();
	  };
	  var _setText = function($button, label) {
	    if ($button.children().length) {
	      $button.children().each(function() {
	        if ($.trim($(this).text()) !== '') {
	          $(this).text(label);
	        }
	      });
	    }
	    else {
	      $button.val(label).text(label);
	    }
	  };

	  var addToCart = function(e, conf) {
      e && e.preventDefault();
      var $addToCartForm = $(this);
      var data = {};
      if (!conf || !conf.product) {
        data = $addToCartForm.serialize();
        conf = _config;
      } else {
        data = conf.product;
      }
      var $addToCartBtn = $addToCartForm.find(conf.addToCartBtnSelector);
			var $addToCartBtnText = $addToCartBtn[0].innerText;

      _setText($addToCartBtn, conf.addingToCartBtnLabel);
      $addToCartBtn.addClass('disabled').prop('disabled', true);
      // Add to cart.
      $.ajax({
        url: conf.shopifyAjaxAddURL,
        dataType: 'json',
        type: 'post',
        data,
        success: function(itemData) {
        // Re-enable add to cart button.
        $addToCartBtn.addClass('inverted');
        _setText($addToCartBtn, conf.addedToCartBtnLabel);
        //_showFeedback('success','<i class="fa fa-check"></i> Added to cart! <a href="/cart">View cart</a>.',$addToCartForm);
        if($('.ajax_success').length < 1){
          _showFeedback('success','<div class="ajax_success"><i class="fa fa-check"></i> Added to cart!</div>',$addToCartForm);
          setTimeout(function(){
            $('.ajax_success').stop(true,true).fadeOut(500)
          },7000);
        }else{
          $('.ajax_success').stop(true,true).fadeIn(500).delay(7000).fadeOut(500);
        }
        window.setTimeout(function(){
          $addToCartBtn.prop('disabled', false).removeClass('disabled').removeClass('inverted');
          _setText($addToCartBtn, $addToCartBtnText);
        }, conf.howLongTillBtnReturnsToNormal);
        // Update cart count and show cart link.
        $.getJSON(conf.shopifyAjaxCartURL, function(cart) {
          
          $(cart.items).each(function(i,v){
            var found = false;
            $('.nav-cart .cart-items li').each(function(p,t){
              if($(this).find('a').attr('href').indexOf(v.variant_id) >= 0){
                $(this).find('.item-subtitle').text('QTY: '+v.quantity)
                found = true;
              }
            })
            if(!found){
              if($('.gn-cart-content .cart-items').length < 1){
                $('.gn-cart-content').html('<ul class="cart-items"></ul>');
              }
              
              $('.gn-cart-content .cart-items').prepend('<li><a class="cart-item" href="'+v.url+'"><span class="item-icon"><img src="'+v.image+'"></span><span class="item-text"><span class="item-title">'+v.product_title+'</span><span class="item-subtitle">QTY: 1</span></span></a></li>')
            }
          })

          $('#AddToCart-product-template').addClass('added');
          $('.cart-qty.header-icon.icon-shopping-cart').addClass('has-items-in-cart').attr('data-content',cart.item_count);
          $('.gn-cart-buttons').css({display:'flex'})
          $('.nav-cart.nav-dropdown--container').stop(true,true).addClass('open')
          setTimeout(function(){
            $('.nav-cart.nav-dropdown--container').stop(true,true).removeClass('open')
          },5000);
          
          if (conf.cartCountSelector && $(conf.cartCountSelector).size()) {
            var value = $(conf.cartCountSelector).html() || '0';
            $(conf.cartCountSelector).html(value.replace(/[0-9]+/,cart.item_count)).removeClass('hidden-count');
          }
          if (conf.cartTotalSelector && $(conf.cartTotalSelector).size()) {
            if (typeof Currency !== 'undefined' && typeof Currency.moneyFormats !== 'undefined') {
              var newCurrency = '';
              if ($('[name="currencies"]').size()) {
              newCurrency = $('[name="currencies"]').val();
              }
              else if ($('#currencies span.selected').size()) {
              newCurrency = $('#currencies span.selected').attr('data-currency');
              }
              if (newCurrency) {
              $(conf.cartTotalSelector).html('<span class=money>' + Shopify.formatMoney(Currency.convert(cart.total_price, "USD", newCurrency), Currency.money_format[newCurrency]) + '</span>');
              } 
              else {
              $(conf.cartTotalSelector).html(Shopify.formatMoney(cart.total_price, "${{amount}}"));
              }
            }
            else {
              $(conf.cartTotalSelector).html(Shopify.formatMoney(cart.total_price, "${{amount}}"));
            }
          };
        });        
        }, 
        error: function(XMLHttpRequest) {
        var response = eval('(' + XMLHttpRequest.responseText + ')');
        response = response.description;
        if (response.slice(0,4) === 'All ') {
          _showFeedback('error', response.replace('All 1 ', 'All '), $addToCartForm);
          $addToCartBtn.prop('disabled', false);
          _setText($addToCartBtn, _config.soldOutBtnLabel);
          $addToCartBtn.prop('disabled',true);
        }
        else {
          _showFeedback('error', '<i class="fa fa-warning"></i> ' + response, $addToCartForm);
          $addToCartBtn.prop('disabled', false).removeClass('disabled');
          _setText($addToCartBtn, _config.addToCartBtnLabel);
        }
        }
      });   
      return false;    
	  }

	  var _init = function() {   
	    $(document).ready(function() { 
	      $(_config.addToCartFormSelector).submit(addToCart);
	    });
	  };
	  return {
	    init: function(params) {
	        // Configuration
	        params = params || {};
	        // Merging with defaults.
	        $.extend(_config, params);
	        // Action
	        $(function() {
	          _init();
	        });
	    },    
	    getConfig: function() {
	      return _config;
	    },
      addToCart: function(params) {
        config = Object.assign(_config, params);
        addToCart.call(this, null, config);
      },
	  }  
	})(jQuery);
	
	Shopify.AjaxifyCart.init();
	</script>

  const THANK_YOU_PAGE_REGEX = /.*?\/checkouts\/.*?\/thank_you.*/;
  const ORDERS_PAGE_REGEX = /.*?\/orders\/.+/;

  function shouldPushPurchaseAmazon() {
    const pushedOrder = sessionStorage.getItem('amzn-pushed-order');
    const thisOrder = '';
    sessionStorage.setItem('amzn-pushed-order', thisOrder);
    return !pushedOrder || pushedOrder !== thisOrder;
  }

  function handleAmznPages(){
    function handleCheckout(){
        const transactionId = new Date().getTime().toString();

        
        const currencyCode = 'USD';            
        

        function pushPurchase(){
            let discountsCodes = [], discountsTotal = 0.0;
            

            amzn('trackEvent', 'order_completed', {
                transaction_id: transactionId,
                shipping_method: '',
                shipping_price: 0.0,
                taxes: 0.0,
                subtotal_price: parseFloat(0.0),
                value: parseFloat(0.0),
                coupon_code: discountsCodes.join(','),
                discount: discountsTotal,
                payment_method: document.querySelector('.payment-icon span').innerText
            });

            amzn('trackEvent', 'Purchase', {
                value: parseFloat('0.0' || '0'),
                unitsSold: parseInt('' || '0'),
                currencyCode
            });
        }

        function pushProducts(){
            
        }

        if(shouldPushPurchaseAmazon()) {
            pushPurchase();
            pushProducts();
        }
    }

    const handlers = [
        { location: THANK_YOU_PAGE_REGEX, handleFunction: handleCheckout },
        { location: ORDERS_PAGE_REGEX, handleFunction: handleCheckout }
    ];

    handlers.forEach(function eachHandler(handler){
        // in a sell operation, order page will be coming from the same domain
        // in case of of coming from an email or orders page, events should not trigger
        if(window.location.href.match(handler.location) !== null
            && document.referrer.includes(window.location.host)) {
            try {
                handler.handleFunction();
            } catch(e){}
        }
    });
  }

  function getPageViewData() {
    const { href } = window.location;

    if(href.match(THANK_YOU_PAGE_REGEX) || href.match(ORDERS_PAGE_REGEX)) {
      return "Thank You"
    }

    return window.document.title;
  }

function setupCampaignDecidedListener() {
  window.optimizely = window.optimizely || [];
  window.optimizely.push({
    type: 'addListener',
    filter: {
      type: 'lifecycle',
      name: 'campaignDecided'
    },
    handler: function(event) {
      try {
        var campaign = event.data.campaign.experiments[0];
        var variationId = event.data.decision.variationId;
        var selectedVariation = event.data.campaign.experiments[0].variations.filter(function(variation) {
          return variation.id === variationId;
        })[0];
        
        var opzCampaignEvent = {
          ['Optimizely: ' + campaign.name]: selectedVariation.name,
          'optimizely_campaign_id': campaign.id,
          'optimizely_campaign_name': campaign.name,
          'optimizely_variation_id': selectedVariation.id,
          'optimizely_variation_name': selectedVariation.name
        };

        //wait for heap
        var interval = setInterval(function() {
          if(window.heap) {
            window.heap.track('optimizely_campaign_decided', opzCampaignEvent);
            clearInterval(interval);
          }
        }, 200);
      } catch(error) {}
    }
  });
}

<script>

  const acecOrigin = 'https://rc3.ring.com';
  const acecCampaign = window.acecCampaign;

  class AmazonConnectEnabledChat {
    
    constructor(el) {
      this.activeClassName = 'acec-container--active';
      this.visibleClassName = 'acec-container--visible';
      this.deactivateChat = 'DEACTIVATE_CHAT';

      this.acecContainer = el;
      this.urlOrigin = acecOrigin;

      // Setup child border / iframe
      const border = document.createElement('div');
      border.classList.add('acec-container__border');

      const iframe = document.createElement('iframe');
      iframe.classList.add('acec-container__iframe');

      const iframeUrl = new URL(`${this.urlOrigin}/nx/chat`);
      iframeUrl.searchParams.append('campaign', acecCampaign);
      iframe.src = iframeUrl.href;

      this.acecIframe = iframe;
      this.acecBorder = border;

      border.appendChild(iframe);
      this.acecContainer.appendChild(border);

      // Setup event listeners
      this.acecContainer.addEventListener('click', () => this.onClick());
      this.acecIframe.onload = this.sendActive(true);
      window.addEventListener('message', (evt) => this.handleMessage(evt));
    }

    onClick() {
      this.sendActive(true);
      this.expand();
    }

    // Expands the chat window
    expand() { this.acecContainer.classList.add(this.activeClassName); }
    
    // Minimizes the chat window
    minimize() { this.acecContainer.classList.remove(this.activeClassName); }
    
    // Remove the chat bubble from page
    hide() { this.acecContainer.classList.remove(this.visibleClassName); }
    
    // Show the chat bubble on page
    show() { this.acecContainer.classList.add(this.visibleClassName); }

    // Handle messages from chat iframe
    handleMessage(event) {
      const { data } = event;
      if (data === this.deactivateChat) this.minimize();
    }

    sendActive(isActive) {
      this.acecIframe.contentWindow.postMessage({ active: isActive }, '*');
    }
  }
  
  function addAcec() {
    //apppend acec container
    const consentBody = document.querySelector('.consent-body');
    const el = document.createElement('div');
    el.classList.add('acec-container');
    consentBody.appendChild(el);

    window.isLaunched = function(launched) {
      if (launched)  { 
        window.acec.show(); 
      } else window.acec.hide();
    }

    window.init = function() {
      window.acec.expand();
    }

    window.acec = new AmazonConnectEnabledChat(el);
  }

  if(window.RC3Enabled) {
    addAcec();
  }
</script>
<!-- End of ACEC snippet -->

        </p>
        
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

<script>
    function openGenericModal(modalID){
      document.querySelector(modalID).classList.add('open');
    };

    // close modal
    const closeGenericModal = document.querySelector('#modal_close_self_cancelation_modal');
    closeGenericModal.addEventListener('click', function(){
      document.querySelector('.ring-generic-modal').classList.toggle('open');
    })
</script>

<script>
  // Get the cookies and see if they are coming from NZ
  const modalNZUsers = document.querySelector('#disclaimer-users-from-nz')

  if(getCookieNZValue('rs_geo')){
    var modalCookie = getCookie('nz_modal_opened');
    if (modalCookie == false){
      modalNZUsers.classList.toggle('open');
      document.cookie = "nz_modal_opened=true";
    };
  };

  // We close the modal on Accept
  document.querySelector('#disclaimer-users-from-nz .ring-generic-modal__accept-continue-button').addEventListener('click', function(){
    modalNZUsers.classList.toggle('open');
  })

</script>

</body>
</html>
